            var rawCookies = document.cookie ? document.cookie.split(";") : [];

                try { cookies[key] = decodeURIComponent(val); } catch { cookies[key] = val; }
              }

            var theme = cookies["theme"];
            var mode = cookies["mode"];
            if (theme) {
              document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-color", theme);
            }

              document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-theme", mode);
            } else {
              var prefersDark = false;
              try {

              } catch {}

bis_skin_checked="1"><p class="text-ui paragraph-lg">🎣 Fish, earn, and compete! Economy bot with Dynamic Economy, Ai Chatbot and Fishing!</p><hr class="h-px! bg-ui/10 border-none! w-full"><div class="entity-content-wrapper w-full" bis_skin_checked="1"><p>FishR is your go-to Discord economy bot with a playful twist. Catch fish, earn credits, level up your score, and grab rare boosts from the shop.</p>
<p>🎣 Fishing Minigame: Cast your line, catch fish, and try to snag rare boosts like Fish Madness for 4x fish!</p>
<p>💰 Dynamic Economy: Sell your fish for credits at a rate that changes every 5 minutes. Watch the market, maximize your gains, and build your wealth.</p>
<p>🏦 Bank &amp; Transactions: Deposit, withdraw, or attempt to steal from friends—strategy and luck combine!</p>
<p>🎯 Score Farm: Solve fast math questions to earn points, but watch out for distractions.</p>
<p>💎 Treasure Chests: Wild chests appear in active chats, giving you coins and fish if you’re quick enough.</p>
<p>FishR is designed to be fast, fun, and full of surprises. Perfect for communities who love casual games, friendly competition, and a bit of chaos.</p>
